## user

Timestamp: 2026-05-15T19:57:47.917Z

Continue Milestone 4: Framework Detection And Repo Fingerprint.

Read docs/milestones/04-framework-detection-and-repo-fingerprint/README.md first, then inspect the current scanner/sample-loader outputs and existing tests before editing. Implement deterministic framework detection and repo fingerprinting so the app can answer: “what kind of codebase is this?”

Goal:
Turn a scanned file inventory into a clear, cautious project fingerprint for the Overview tab.

Required files to create or update:
- repoquest/framework_rules.py
- repoquest/detectors.py
- tests/test_detectors.py

Implementation requirements:
- Detect frameworks using deterministic evidence, not guesses.
- Detect React/Vite.
- Detect Next.js.
- Detect Express.
- Detect FastAPI.
- Detect Flask.
- Detect Streamlit.
- Detect Django.
- Detect Python packages.
- Detect CLI/tooling projects.
- Classify project type with confidence.
- Detect and rank likely entry points.
- Detect key folders.
- Return evidence strings for every framework finding.
- Use cautious language when confidence is low.
- Do not claim certainty unless file evidence supports it.

Expected fingerprint output should support:
- project type
- confidence
- frameworks
- entry points
- key folders
- warnings

Tests to add or update:
- Demo repo detects React/Vite.
- Demo repo detects FastAPI.
- Demo repo is classified as a full-stack web application.
- Streamlit fixture detects Streamlit.
- Unknown fixture falls back without overclaiming.
- Entry point detection includes at least one frontend and one backend entry point for the demo repo.

Design guidance:
Keep rules explicit and auditable. Prefer simple rule tables in framework_rules.py and detection orchestration in detectors.py. Each framework result should include name, confidence or strength, and evidence strings such as package files, config files, imports, or known entry files. Avoid heuristic overreach; unknown or weak evidence should produce warnings or low confidence instead of confident claims.

Before finishing:
- Run the relevant tests.
- Report changed files.
- Report test results.
- Include a short example of the demo repo fingerprint.
- Mention any limitations or follow-up needed for the Overview tab.

Exit criteria:
The demo repo fingerprint clearly identifies it as a React/Vite + FastAPI full-stack web application, and the Overview tab has enough structured data to show project type, confidence, frameworks, entry points, keyand warnings.

Remove ignored directories from traversal\n        dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if not should_ignore_path(os.path.join(root, d))]\n        \n        for filename in filenames:\n            total_seen += 1\n            \n            if total_scanned >= MAX_FILES_SCANNED:\n                warnings.append(f\"Reached max file limit ({MAX_FILES_SCANNED}). return a repository snapshot.\n    \n    Args:\n        zip_path: Path to the ZIP file\n        \n    Returns:\n        RepositorySnapshot with scanned files and warnings\n        \n    Raises:\n Check if path should be ignored\n                if should_ignore_path(entry):\n                    continue\n                \n                # Get entry info\n                try:\n                    info = zf.getinfo(entry)\n                except KeyError:\n                    warnings.append(f\"Cannot access ZIP entry '{entry}'\")\n                    continue\n                \n                # Check if should skip\n                should_skip, skip_reason = should_skip_zip_entry(entry, info.file_size)\n                \n                entry_path = Path(entry)\n                suffix = entry_path.suffix.lower()\n                language = LANGUAGE_MAP.get(suffix, \"Unknown\")\n                \n                if should_skip:\n                    files.append(FileInfo(\n                        path=entry,\n                        name=entry_path.name,\n                        suffix=suffix,\n                        size_bytes=info.file_size,\n                        language=language,\n                        role=\"skipped\",\n                        text_preview=\"\",\n                        line_count=0,\n                        skipped=True,\n                        skip_reason=skip_reason,\n                    ))\n                    continue\n                \n                # Read and process file content\n                try:\n                    content_bytes = safe_read_zip_entry(zf, entry, MAX_FILE_SIZE_BYTES)\n                    text_preview, line_count = extract_text_preview_from_bytes(content_bytes)\n                    role = guess_file_role(entry_path)\n                    \n                    files.append(FileInfo(\n                        path=entry,\n                        name=entry_path.name,\n                        suffix=suffix,\n                        size_bytes=info.file_size,\n                        language=language,\n                        role=role,\n                        text_preview=text_preview,\n                        line_count=line_count,\n                        skipped=False,\n                        skip_reason=None,\n                    ))\n                    \n                    total_scanned += 1\n                except ZIPSafetyError as e:\n                    warnings.append(f\"Cannot read '{entry}': {e}\")\n                    continue\n    \n    except zipfile.BadZipFile as e:\n        raise ZIPSafetyError(f\"Corrupted ZIP file: {e}\")\n    except Exception as e:\n        if isinstance(e, ZIPSafetyError):\n            raise\n        raise ZIPSafetyError(f\"ZIP scanning failed: {e}\")\n    \n    return RepositorySnapshot(\n        source_name=zip_path.name,\n        files=files,\n        total_files_seen=total_seen,\n        total_files_scanned=total_scanned,\n        warnings=warnings,\n    )\n\n# Made with Bob"
```json
          }
        }
      }
    ],
    "status": "success",
    "timestamp": "2026-05-15T19:58:01.355Z",
    "resultDisplay": "",
    "displayName": "ReadFile",
    "description": "Reads and returns the content of a specified file. If the file is large, the content will be truncated. The tool's response will clearly indicate if truncation has occurred and will provide details on how to read more of the file using the 'offset' and 'limit' parameters. Handles text, images (PNG, JPG, GIF, WEBP, SVG, BMP), and PDF files. For text files, it can read specific line ranges.",
    "renderOutputAsMarkdown": true
  }
]
```

<summary>Tool calls</summary>

```json
[
  {
    "id": "tool-41",
    "name": "write_to_file",
    "args": {
      "file_path": "/home/ovidiu/Projects/bob/proj/repoquest/detectors.py",
      "content": "\"\"\"Framework detection and project fingerprinting for RepoQuest.\n\nThis module orchestrates framework detection using the rules defined in framework_rules.py\nand produces a ProjectFingerprint that answers \"what kind of codebase is this?\"\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom repoquest.models import (\n    RepositorySnapshot,\n    FileInfo,\n    FrameworkFinding,\n    ProjectFingerprint,\n)\nfrom repoquest.framework_rules import (\n    ALL_FRAMEWORK_RULES,\n    FrameworkRule,\n    ENTRY_POINT_PATTERNS,\n    classify_project_type,\n    KEY_FOLDERS,\n)\n\n\ndef detect_framework(rule: FrameworkRule, snapshot: RepositorySnapshot) -> FrameworkFinding | None:\n    \"\"\"Detect a framework using a specific rule.\n    \n    Args:\n        rule: The framework detection rule to apply\n        snapshot: The repository snapshot to analyze\n        \n    Returns:\n        FrameworkFinding if detected with sufficient confidence, None otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    evidence = []\n    confidence = 0.0\n    found_any_evidence = False\n    \n    # Check for required files (must have ALL)\n    if rule.required_files:\n        required_found = all(\n            any(f.name == req_file for f in snapshot.files)\n            for req_file in rule.required_files\n        )\n        if not required_found:\n            return None  # Missing required files, framework not present\n    \n    # Check for indicator files (having ANY increases confidence)\n    if rule.indicator_files:\n        for indicator_file in rule.indicator_files:\n            for file in snapshot.files:\n                if file.name == indicator_file:\n                    evidence.append(f\"Found {indicator_file}\")\n                    confidence += rule.file_match_boost\n                    found_any_evidence = True\n    \n    # Check for content patterns\n    if rule.content_patterns:\n        for pattern in rule.content_patterns:\n            for file in snapshot.files:\n                if file.skipped:\n                    continue\n                if pattern.lower() in file.text_preview.lower():\n                    evidence.append(f\"Found '{pattern}' in {file.name}\")\n                    confidence += rule.content_match_boost\n                    found_any_evidence = True\n                    break  # Only count each pattern once\n    \n    # Check for indicator paths\n    if rule.indicator_paths:\n        for indicator_path in rule.indicator_paths:\n            for file in snapshot.files:\n                if indicator_path.lower() in file.path.lower():\n                    evidence.append(f\"Found path pattern '{indicator_path}'\")\n                    confidence += rule.path_match_boost\n                    found_any_evidence = True\n                    break  # Only count each path pattern once\n    \n    # If we found any evidence, add base confidence\n    if found_any_evidence:\n        confidence += rule.base_confidence\n    \n    # Cap confidence at 1.0\n    confidence = min(confidence, 1.0)\n    \n    # Only return if we have meaningful confidence (>= 0.3)\n    if confidence >= 0.3 and evidence:\n        return FrameworkFinding(\n            name=rule.name,\n            category=rule.category,\n            confidence=confidence,\n            evidence=evidence[:5],  # Limit evidence to top 5 items\n        )\n    \n    return None\n\n\ndef detect_entry_points(snapshot: RepositorySnapshot) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Detect likely entry points in the repository.\n    \n    Args:\n        snapshot: The repository snapshot to analyze\n        \n    Returns:\n        List of entry point paths with descriptions\n    \"\"\"\n    entry_points = []\n    \n    for file in snapshot.files:\n        if file.skipped:\n            continue\n        \n        # Check against known entry point patterns\n        for pattern, description in ENTRY_POINT_PATTERNS:\n            if file.path.endswith(pattern) or pattern in file.path:\n                entry_points.append(f\"{file.path} ({description})\")\n                break\n    \n    # Sort by likely importance (backend first, then frontend)\n    def entry_point_priority(ep: str) -> int:\n        ep_lower = ep.lower()\n        if \"backend\" in ep_lower or \"main.py\" in ep_lower:\n            return 0\n        if \"frontend\" in ep_lower or \"app.tsx\" in ep_lower:\n            return 1\n        if \"streamlit\" in ep_lower:\n            return 2\n        return 3\n    \n    entry_points.sort(key=entry_point_priority)\n    \n    return entry_points\n\n\ndef detect_key_folders(snapshot: RepositorySnapshot) -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Detect key folders in the repository.\n    \n    Args:\n        snapshot: The repository snapshot to analyze\n        \n    Returns:\n        List of key folder paths with descriptions\n    \"\"\"\n    found_folders = set()\n    key_folder_list = []\n    \n    for file in snapshot.files:\n        path_parts = Path(file.path).parts\n        \n        # Check each part of the path\n        for part in path_parts[:-1]:  # Exclude the filename itself\n            folder_key = part + \"/\"\n            if folder_key in KEY_FOLDERS and folder_key not in found_folders:\n                found_folders.add(folder_key)\n                key_folder_list.append(f\"{folder_key} ({KEY_FOLDERS[folder_key]})\")\n    \n    return sorted(key_folder_list)\n\n\ndef generate_fingerprint(snapshot: RepositorySnapshot) -> ProjectFingerprint:\n    \"\"\"Generate a project fingerprint from a repository snapshot.\n    \n    This is the main entry point for framework detection and project classification.\n    \n    Args:\n        snapshot: The repository snapshot to analyze\n        \n    Returns:\n        ProjectFingerprint with detected frameworks, project type, and metadata\n    \"\"\"\n    warnings = list(snapshot.warnings)  # Copy warnings from snapshot\n    \n    # Detect all frameworks\n    frameworks = []\n    for rule in ALL_FRAMEWORK_RULES:\n        finding = detect_framework(rule, snapshot)\n        if finding:\n            frameworks.append(finding)\n    \n    # Sort frameworks by confidence (highest first)\n    frameworks.sort(key=lambda f: f.confidence, reverse=True)\n    \n    # Detect entry points\n    entry_points = detect_entry_points(snapshot)\n    \n    # Detect key folders\n    key_folders = detect_key_folders(snapshot)\n    \n    # Classify project type\n    framework_names = [f.name for f in frameworks]\n    project_type, type_confidence = classify_project_type(framework_names, entry_points)\n    \n    # Generate summary\n    if frameworks:\n        top_frameworks = \", \".join(f.name for f in frameworks[:3])\n        summary = f\"Detected as {project_type} with {top_frameworks}\"\n    else:\n        summary = f\"Classified as {project_type} with limited framework detection\"\n        warnings.append(\"RepoQuest could not confidently detect specific frameworks\")\n    \n    # Add warnings for low confidence\n    if type_confidence < 0.5:\n        warnings.append(\n            \"RepoQuest could not confidently classify this repo, \"\n            \"but it found these likely entry points and important files\"\n        )\n    \n    # Add warning if no entry points found\n    if not entry_points:\n        warnings.append(\"No standard entry points detected\")\n    \n    return ProjectFingerprint(\n        project_type=project_type,\n        confidence=type_confidence,\n        frameworks=frameworks,\n        entry_points=entry_points,\n        key_folders=key_folders,\n        summary=summary,\n        warnings=warnings,\n    )\n\n# Made with Bob\n"
    },
    "result": [
```
